Xuzhou and Haizhou 56

Regarding the Proposition to Divide the Provincial Districts

The History, Geography, Transportation, and Customs of the Two Regions Are the Same

Telegraph to the Central Government Not to Separately Divide the Two Regions

Xuzhou correspondence: Representatives of the party departments of the twelve counties in Xuzhou and Haizhou recently met in Xuzhou to discuss the issue of dividing the provincial districts of Xuzhou and Haizhou. As a result of the discussion, it was considered that there was an indispensable need for the two regions of Xuzhou and Haizhou to be undivided in terms of history, geography, transportation, and customs. Today (7th), they telegraphed the central party department, the national government, and the national assembly, requesting that Xuzhou and Haizhou be classified as one province, supplemented by the counties in Eastern Henan, Northern Anhui, and Southern Shandong, totaling twenty-nine counties, to form a province to conform to popular sentiment and facilitate administration. The telegram reads: "Since the Three Dynasties, our country has been plagued by continuous turmoil and repeated warfare. Whether on a national or local scale, there have rarely been periods of several hundred years without conflict. Tracing the origin of the disasters, it is generally due to the excessive size of the divided provinces and districts, making measures difficult to implement, which has gradually evolved into a separatist situation. Our central government, in view of this, and for the sake of ending war and promoting peace, has proposed the idea of dividing the country into sixty-nine provinces. Upon hearing this, we were overjoyed. Recently, we heard rumors that Xuzhou would be assigned to Guide province and Haizhou would be assigned to Huaihai province. If this is true, the central government may have other good plans, but Xuzhou and Haizhou have close relations in history, geography, and popular customs, and there is an inseparable trend. We have to briefly state it: Examining the division of the nine provinces by Xia Yu, Haidai and Huai were Xuzhou, and the governor of Xuzhou in the Later Han Dynasty governed Tan, and Haizhou was the state of Tan. In the third year of the Republic of China, Xuzhou Daoyin was established. Historically speaking, Xuzhou and Haizhou were originally one family, and it seems inappropriate to separate them. First, in terms of geography, Xuzhou and Haizhou are located at the same latitude of 35 degrees north, and their territories are adjacent and rivers intersect, so it seems inappropriate to separate them. Second, the Longhai Railway runs directly through Xuzhou. In the future, when the Haizhou commercial port is completed, Xuzhou and Haizhou will be no different from a gate and a hall. The so-called lips and teeth are interdependent, so it seems inappropriate to separate them in terms of situation and transportation. Third, furthermore, Xuzhou and Haizhou have the same climate, and their customs and habits are completely similar. If they can be classified as one province, there will be no risk of obstacles in future administrative measures. This is the fourth reason why it is impossible to separate them in terms of popular customs. Now that our party has unified the country, all ethnic prejudices and feudal ideas should be completely eliminated, and there should be no distinction between this boundary and that boundary. However, for the sake of administrative convenience, it seems appropriate to give due consideration. Although Xuzhou and Guide are adjacent, they belong to two provinces. Is it not because their customs and habits are different and their popular sentiments are also different? The political measures of Jiangsu and Henan provinces are all governed separately. Moreover, the people of the two provinces have had border disputes, which have been incompatible for a long time. If the people who cannot tolerate each other are classified as one province, the administrative obstacles will be difficult to escape. It would be better for Xuzhou and Haizhou to be the same province, the same road, the same customs and the same popular sentiments. The people of Xuzhou and Haizhou have seen this and held a meeting on April 8 at the Tongshan County Party Department. The representatives of the twelve counties who attended the meeting resolved to telegraph the Central Party Department, the National Government, and the National Assembly, requesting that the twelve counties of Xuzhou and Haizhou, as well as Si, Ling, Su, Wo, Hao in Anhui, Yong, Xia, Shangqiu in Henan, Tan, Lin, Fei, Teng, Yu, Jin, Shan, Cao in Shandong, be classified as one province. The reason for this is that it is reasonable to appeal to you to adopt public opinion and approve the request, so as to benefit administration and conform to public sentiment. It is impossible to wait for orders in a hurry (7th).

Split Within the Jiangxi Red Bandit Forces 61

Huang Gonglue Declared Opposition to Zhu

Nanchang Correspondence: The mutual infighting between Zhu De and Mao Zedong has long become irreconcilable. Zhu's bandits even instigated the AB group to riot in Futian, destroying the Futian pseudo-Soviet. Li Shaojiu (Labor and Peasant Commissioner) and Liu Tiechao (pseudo-Commander of the 20th Army) were detained. As a result, Red bandit Huang Gonglue issued a declaration accusing Zhu De of being commanded by the Chen Duxiu of the abolitionist faction, destroying the organization. Now, the Propaganda Department of the General Headquarters has received a copy of Huang's declaration sent by the 40th Division, which shows that the Red bandits have been divided into four or five factions. The declaration roughly states that Duan Liangbi, Li Bofang, Liu Di, Xie Han, Chang Jin, Wanbang, etc., communist party members of the rich peasant and landlord class who claimed to be the revolutionary leaders of Jiangxi, joined the AB group abolitionist faction in an attempt to eliminate the Soviet and eliminate the Red Army. Now that the plot has been leaked, the officers and soldiers of the 20th Army, who were deceived by the AB group Liu Di, mutinied in Donggu, broke into Futian, overthrew the Jiangxi Provincial Soviet Government, destroyed the Jiangxi Provincial Action Committee, released the AB group abolitionist faction leaders Duan Liangbi, Li Bofang, Jin Wanbang and other major criminals, and detained Yi Ershi, the central inspector, Liu Tiechao, the commander of the 20th Army, and Li Shaojiu, the special commissioner of the Chinese Workers and Peasants Revolutionary Committee, and drove away Lu Shan, the chairman of the provincial government. This incident is a conspiracy of the AB group abolitionist faction. I hereby declare as follows: (1) Xie Han, Chang Duan, Liangbi Li, Bofang and others came from the rich peasant and landlord class. For the past two or three years, they have not advocated land distribution. Last year, at the 27th joint meeting, under the leadership of Liu Shiqi and others, they reluctantly implemented land distribution. In July, at the Second Plenary Session of the Ganxi Southwest Special Committee, Duan Liangbi and others, in the name of the central government, opposed land distribution by pretexting the transformation of peasant consciousness, abused the slogan of centralized armed forces, and did not leave a single gun, becoming the Red Army of the AB group and implementing class struggle. They wanted to send the Red Army to the white area to eliminate them. At the same time, they greatly developed organizations in various counties and arranged counter-revolutionary riots, and sent the AB group abolitionist faction to infiltrate the Red Army in the name of expanding the Red Army, secretly making white flags, and scheduled riots. Duan Liangbi, Li Bofang, Jin Wanbang and others were arrested at that time and personally confessed that they were the leaders of the AB group. They took the theory of the abolitionist faction on the outside and secretly did the practical work of the AB group in government agencies and parties. It was completely a counter-revolutionary conspiracy under the command of Chen Duxiu. (2) The Futian Incident is the total riot of the AB group abolitionist faction in openly counter-revolution. Their conspiracy is to abolish the land revolution, eliminate the Soviet, eliminate the Red Army, suppress the poor workers and peasants, and attempt to split the revolutionary forces with the slogan of defeating Mao Zedong and supporting Zhu Peng Huang.

Qingdao Business Tax Implementation Nears 62

Qingdao Correspondence: The Qingdao Business Tax Preparatory Committee dispatched personnel to investigate everything, and it is mostly completed. The committee held its ninth meeting on the 6th, chaired by Guo Binghe. The discussion items included: 1. The Finance Bureau proposed a draft amendment to the implementation rules of the Business Tax Regulations, which was resolved to be retained. 2. The Finance Bureau proposed a revised plan for the Business Tax Assessment Standards and Tax Rate Table, which was resolved to be amended and passed. 3. The Second Section proposed requests from various trade associations for tax reduction or exemption from business tax or for amendment of tax rates, which was resolved that the tax rates have been reviewed and revised, and will be submitted to the central government for approval. In addition, the committee has discussed the method of collecting business tax several times, and solicited the opinions of various members for adoption. The date of implementation is probably not far away.

The Finance Bureau received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance yesterday, explaining the scope of business tax exemption: 1. Wholesale businesses directly established by construction companies are exempt from business tax, but commercial firms and shops that promote and sell are still subject to tax. 2. Zhuang households that only buy and do not sell, and have no business income, may be exempt from business tax. (May 7)

Survey of Sutra Collections in Shandong 63

Buddhist Sutras are more numerous, Daoist Sutras are the fewest.

The Sutra Collection of Laoshan is perfectly preserved.

Jinan Correspondence: Since the Great Sutra Collection of Hainan Temple in Yexian County was damaged, the Shandong Department of Education sent personnel to investigate and transported the remaining books to Jinan for preservation. Subsequently, there was news of the loss of the Great Sutra Collection of Shijia Temple in Jiyang County. The Department of Education again sent the County Education Bureau to investigate nearby. Sutra Collections are a grand spectacle of Chinese documents, and many temples in northern provinces have numerous collections. Shandong also has many Sutra Collections. According to Wang Xiantang, the director of the Shandong Library, Sutra Collections are divided into two types: the Great Sutra (i.e., Buddhist Sutras) and Daoist Sutras. The temples in Shandong mostly preserve Buddhist Sutras, and Daoist Sutras are the fewest. The collection of Hainan Temple in Yexian County is the Ming Dynasty version of the Great Sutra, which has now been transported to the library. Qianfo Temple in Yexian County still has half of the Ming Dynasty version, which is very well preserved. Jiyang has a complete Ming Dynasty version, which is said to have been lost, and is currently under investigation. A private collection of half of the Ming Dynasty version exists on Shunhuang Temple Street in Jinan (it is said that the book owner is named Wu). In addition, Jingju Temple outside the East Gate of Jinan has a complete collection of the new version of the Great Sutra, which was donated by Pan Yunhang. As for Daoist Sutras, the Shandong Library has an incomplete Ming Dynasty version. It is said that Laoshan has a complete Ming Dynasty version, which is very well preserved. According to the Four Libraries Summary, there are four printed versions of the Great Sutra in China: two Chinese versions (Zheng and Xu), one Japanese version, and one Korean version. The Showa Great Sutra currently being printed in Japan is a combined edition of the above four versions.

National Qingdao University sent Bo Jun to Laoshan to investigate the Sutra Collections of Taiqing Palace and Huayan Temple. Ding Jun has already submitted a written report, stating that he inspected the Daoist and Great Sutra Collections of Taiqing Palace and Huayan Temple in Laoshan on May 2nd and 3rd, accompanied by the two deans, Wen and Huang, and inquired about everything. It is said that they are well preserved. According to the Four Libraries Summary, the Daoist Sutras were compiled by Bai Yunjii in the Ming Dynasty and completed in the year of Bingyin of the Tianqi era. Bai's detailed notes on the Daoist Sutra catalog include more than 1,400 types. During the Wanli period, 50 types were added, totaling more than 1,500 types. Now, the collection in the main hall of Taiqing Palace is the edition promulgated by imperial decree in the 35th year of Wanli of the Ming Dynasty. Randomly examining one type, the Panxi Collection, the Wanli year of Wuxu is printed in the dragon pattern at the end of the volume. It is finely printed on Xuan paper and bound in brocade. The promulgated imperial edict is still engraved and stored. According to the abbot, the entire collection has more than 4,000 volumes, which is also mentioned in Ding Shuzhi's Travels in Laoshan, seemingly inconsistent with Bai's catalog. The Great Sutra, located in Huayan Temple, was presented in Beijing in the eighth year of Qianlong and is a printed edition from the early years of Yongzheng. According to the Essentials of Series Books, based on the edition of the Hongjiao Bookstore in Japan, there are a total of 1,916 volumes. The abbot of the temple said that there are more than 700 volumes, and because they are not lent out, they are said to be complete. The Sutra Pavilion also contains many other Sutras. Random checks reveal that most are printed editions from the Zhengtong and Xuande eras, and there are also many Confucian classics, which do not seem to be highly valued. Daoist and Buddhist Sutras are grand spectacles of our country's documents. Few survive, and even fewer are complete. The catalogs of various families generally do not contain detailed information. Yang Shoujing was knowledgeable in various books and was considered the best of his time. The Essentials of Series Books he wrote only covers the Japanese edition of the Great Sutra and only covers the summary of the Daoist Sutras. The Tianqi Bingyin edition does not include the Wanli continuation, so it seems that he did not see the entire collection. Therefore, these two books are almost unique in China, and their value is estimated to be more than hundreds of millions. (May 8)

Wuhu Express 64

The National Government Supervisory Yuan previously sent Councilor Shang Wenli to Anhui to investigate the situation of various taxes after the abolition of Likin, and to investigate the 1 million yuan rice and grain public bond recently raised in Anhui Province. Shang stayed in Wuhu for several days and took a boat to Datong on the morning of the 8th, and then went to Anqing from Datong.

The business tax in Anhui Province is still under preparation. Wuhu merchants recently put forward opinions, unanimously requesting: 1. Rice and grain are tax-free goods, and request exemption from taxation. 2. Tobacco, alcohol, kerosene, and flour have already been taxed with special taxes and should be exempted. 3. Firewood and charcoal are essential for people's livelihood and should be allowed to be taxed at a reduced rate. 4. The date of commencement of taxation should be postponed to June 12.

All circles in Wuhu held a National Humiliation Memorial Meeting at the YMCA at 9:00 am on the National Humiliation Memorial Day on May 9th. At the same time, each school sent three speech teams to give speeches in different directions.

The Wuhu Infant Care Center is poorly managed. According to investigations, there are currently 148 infants in the center, of which 34 suffer from internal and external diseases, and even more suffer from scabies. In order to rectify the situation, Lu Tingzhen has been specially promoted to director, and the Public Security Bureau and the County Government have issued notices to attach 1% of the house rent as a subsidy for the center.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 66

County-wide Boy Scout General Review: The Boy Scouts of this county held a three-day large-scale event at the public sports ground yesterday (9th). A total of six troops, totaling 300 people, attended. At 9:00 am today, Ni Han, the director of the Department of Education, the government secretary, and the Zhengwei, etc. served as inspectors and held a solemn ceremony. The Boy Scouts uniforms were bright, the clothing was neat, and their spirit was very brave. The instructors swiftly issued commands, and the review proceeded smoothly. Wang Jikun, a standing committee member, delivered a speech on behalf of the provincial party headquarters. He stated that Boy Scouts must pay attention to thought and action. In terms of thought, there are three main ideas: the Three Principles of the People, Communism, and Nationalism. However, Communism and Nationalism are not central ideas, and we should all concentrate on the ideas of the Three Principles of the People in order to be accurate. Actions must be disciplined and organized in groups so that we can develop a spirit of service. The speech was thorough and the meeting adjourned after the ceremony.

Wuxi 67

Two Men Commit Suicide Due to Economic Pressure: Zhang Xixian, also known as Genquan, a resident of Shicang outside the South Gate of this county, was 24 years old. He worked as a runner for the Xiechang Oil Company in Shanghai. Recently, Xixian was encouraged by a friend to raise shares and open an oil shop in Chongming County. However, the shop closed down due to losses less than a week after opening. Zhang then returned to Wuxi on the 7th of this month and stayed in room 20 on the upper floor of the Qitai Inn on Tongyun Road, laughing as usual and showing no signs of abnormality. At 9:00 am the day before yesterday (9th), the tea room saw that the guest had not yet gotten up, so he opened the door to check and saw that Zhang Xixian's face was pale and he was lying straight, with only a breath left. He did not respond when called. He realized that he had taken poison and found two empty bottles of "Barbital" sedative pills on the table, as well as two suicide notes. He immediately reported to the accountant and carried him to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. After Dr. Zhu's careful acupuncture treatment, his life may be saved. The reason for his suicide was economic pressure. Hui Hanxiang, a resident of Zhoushanbang, used to be a worker. Recently, he has been unemployed at home, which has made his finances extremely tight. Therefore, he suddenly developed a pessimistic view of life and drank five catties of yellow wine and a large bowl of foreign alkaline water yesterday, instantly falling into a daze and losing consciousness. Later, his family noticed and immediately sent him to the Brothers Hospital for treatment, which allowed him to turn the corner.

Farmhouse Robbed in the Middle of the Night: In the Dongfang Zhuang Shuiqueli area of Zhangjingqiao, Seventh District (Huai Shangshi), Hu Genyu, a resident who works as a blacksmith, is extremely frugal and has some savings. Recently, he also built a Xieshun silkworm house in Dongfangqiao, which was coveted by bandits. At about 2:00 am the night before last, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came to Hu's house, broke into the house with weapons. At that time, Hu's family, big and small, were awakened from their dreams. After the bandits entered the room, they dragged Hu Genyu off the bed, tied him with hemp rope, and beat him severely, forcing him to reveal the location of the hidden silver. Then they ransacked the house for an hour before packing up the stolen goods, carrying them out the door, and fleeing north. After the incident, the loss was estimated to be about 500 yuan. Yesterday, the victim, Hu Genyu, reported the robbery to the police brigade headquarters, which immediately sent detective Hua Yaoxian to the countryside to investigate and apprehend the stolen goods and bandits.

The Case of the Robbery of Zhucui Shan's House is Solved: Wang Wei, the captain of the county police brigade, received a secret report the day before yesterday stating that He Abing and other robbers who robbed the house of Zhu Xingshan near Zhangjingqiao, Seventh District (Huai Shangshi), were now hiding in the Luozhuang area of the district. He was requested to quickly send a team to arrest them. Captain Wang immediately ordered the detective team leader to lead detectives Hua Yaoxian and Hao Zhiliang to the countryside to arrest them at the address. He Abing was arrested on the spot, escorted to the city, and sent to the brigade headquarters. After Captain Wang's detailed interrogation, the suspect confessed to robbing Zhu Xingshan's house and using the stolen goods. Captain Wang immediately ordered him to be temporarily detained pending transfer to the county for interrogation. Qian Tianxiong, the captain of the water patrol team, and Wang Jinbiao, a special agent, also arrested a suspect, Chen Shengquan (i.e., Chen Shengkui), a remnant of the bandit leader Hang Zupei, who was killed in action, in the Miaoxia area the day before yesterday, and immediately escorted him to the brigade headquarters for interrogation.

Nantong 68

The Rickshaw Donation Strike is Difficult to Resolve: The rickshaw pullers in Nantong, because various sections of the road have been in disrepair for a long time, and the Construction Bureau has not repaired them, recently suddenly increased donations. More than a thousand people gathered to oppose the donation increase. The county government's persuasion was ineffective, resulting in the stagnation of rickshaw donations from the Construction Bureau for several months. County Magistrate Zhang submitted a report to the department for instructions. On the 9th, he received instructions stating that the rickshaw pullers in the county had united to resist donations and gathered to coerce the Construction Bureau into reorganizing the rickshaw donations and issuing licenses. The department had not investigated the report, which was already particularly tolerant. The request to reduce rickshaw donations should not be discussed. However, the rickshaw pullers regarded road repairs as a prerequisite, and it is difficult

Jiangyin 69

Notorious Bandit Qin Qiyun from the Eastern Countryside Executed by Firing Squad: Qin Qiyun, a notorious bandit from the eastern countryside, was captured by the Canglin Bridge Security Corps on the 2nd of this month. After being handed over to the county and interrogated, his guilt was confirmed. An official report was telegraphed to the Civil Affairs Bureau, and upon approval by the provincial government, the county government was instructed by telegram on the 8th to execute Qin. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Li ordered the police to bring out the prisoner on the afternoon of the 9th, verified his identity, and escorted him to an open area near the tomb of Yang Mingshi outside the east gate, where he was executed by firing squad.

The Strike is Temporarily Resolved: The merchants and residents of the Hou District, in protest against Huang Zhifang, the head of the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau, for prohibiting theatrical performances and privately punishing Zhu Xianghan and others, initiated a strike that has lasted for two days. County Magistrate Li inspected the district administration and pacified the area, earnestly persuading the people and requesting Branch Head Huang to apologize to the merchants and residents by setting off firecrackers. The merchants and residents resumed business first, and the matter of how to punish Branch Head Huang is still pending as the merchants and residents have telegraphed the provincial authorities and are awaiting instructions from their superiors. The strike has been temporarily resolved.

Yangzhou 70

The Governor's Office Orders Investigation into Concealing Bandits Case: The Pacification Commissioner's Office received a complaint from Zheng Dechang and Li Liangde, residents of Xiaozheng Village and Shiqiao Village, respectively, located at the border of Pi and Tong Counties. They alleged that Shen Jingzhou, the captain of the Second Squad of the Public Security Bureau, was harboring Li Dunrong, a notorious bandit from Taoyuan Village in Tongshan County, by enlisting him as a soldier in the Seventh Platoon under the alias of Li Feng'e. After the complaint, Pi County captured and detained Li Feng'e. A special order was issued to the Pi County government to investigate whether Li Feng'e was indeed the notorious bandit Li Dunrong using an alias, to promptly summon the plaintiffs for questioning and legal action, and to avoid any concealment or leniency. The handling of the case should be reported. Additionally, Zhou Zhenjun, the district chief of the Twelfth District of Tongshan, and Zhou Daochang, the police captain, also reported to the Governor's Office that Hu Yuquan, the district chief of the First District of Pi County, and Zou Yunliang, the police captain, were suspected of harboring and condoning bandits, leading to the persistent activity of Red Bandits in the area. Yesterday (the 8th), the Pi County Magistrate was instructed to investigate and report back, with a deadline for suppressing the Red Bandits in the region.

Hangzhou 71

Jufeng Garden Employee Commits Suicide Due to Illness: Jin Sheng, an employee of the Jufeng Garden Restaurant in Hangzhou, previously served as a cook for the guard team during the West Lake Exposition. After the exposition concluded, Captain Wu, impressed by his loyalty, recommended him to Jufeng Garden as a general worker, a position he held for over a year. The owner, Wang Qingchun, also praised him for his diligence and honesty. However, this spring, Jin Sheng developed an eye ailment and took leave from the restaurant for over half a month. Despite spending a considerable amount on medical expenses, his condition did not improve. Overwhelmed with despair, he decided to end his life and ingested opium yesterday. His roommates discovered him and rushed him to Guangji Hospital for treatment.

Gaoyou 72

Normal School Student Saved After Attempting Suicide by Poisoning: Wu Jiong, a first-year student at the County Normal School located on East Main Street in the city, went to the home of his relative, Zhang, yesterday. For unknown reasons, he secretly ingested opium last night (the 7th) in an attempt to commit suicide. Fortunately, someone noticed him early, and he was rushed to the Dalu Pharmacy on Caiyi Street for emergency treatment, and his life was saved.

Merchant Ship Sinks Coal Boat: A small upstream boat belonging to the China Merchants Bureau was sailing through the Mapeng Bay area of the county yesterday when it collided head-on with a coal boat. The two vessels were unable to avoid each other, resulting in the sinking of the coal boat. Negotiations are currently underway to resolve the matter.

Taizhou 73

Commits Suicide Over Minor Quarrel: The 21-year-old daughter of Wang Zixiang, a resident of Hetou in Linhai City, argued with her cousin's wife over a minor matter yesterday (the 7th). Overwhelmed by the situation, she ingested thirty-two red pills in an attempt to take her own life. After her family discovered her, they hired a doctor to treat her, but it was too late, and she soon died.

Xuzhou 74

Bandit Arrested, Hangs Himself in Jail: The Tongshan County government reported yesterday through Seventh District Chief Liu Chengbin that a bandit, Zhang Chuanyi, had been apprehended by the police and sent to the district. The bandit, fearing punishment and unable to endure his opium addiction, feigned needing to urinate. Taking advantage of a moment of carelessness, he went to the stable and hanged himself. The guards who went to check on him later found him dead. After receiving the report, the county government dispatched Assize Official Huang Jiazhen and a scribe to conduct an autopsy today.

Jiaxing 75

Meeting to Maintain the Silk Industry: The silkworm season in the four rural areas of Jiaxing is approaching, but of the hundred or so cocoon factories in the county, only thirteen have decided to open and operate. Therefore, the Department of Construction specifically ordered prompt measures to be taken to help the farmers. County Magistrate Gong convened a meeting at the County Chamber of Commerce on the afternoon of the 9th, bringing together silk cocoon merchants, financiers, and key figures from various local chambers of commerce to discuss the matter. The following resolutions were reached: (1) Jiaxing financiers will lend 1 million yuan to facilitate circulation, with a 4-6 split for security, following the usual procedures of previous years. (2) A temporary relief committee for silk cocoons will be formed, and Gu Suming, Qian Boying, Zhang Ximin, Shen Jun, Chu Fucheng, Shen Xiping, Wu Heshuyi, Xi Shinong, and Liang Hua will be appointed as members. (3) The relief committee will request the provincial government to waive all cocoon taxes for this year. (4) Factory rents will be limited to 80 yuan per double stove and 40 yuan per single stove, with existing contracts unaffected. (5) Wu Heshuyi and Liang Hua will be tasked with drafting a concrete plan for establishing a public drying kiln, to be discussed at the first relief committee meeting for silk cocoons on the 13th.

Capture of Bandits in the Shawan Robbery Case: After a gang of bandits carried out a large-scale robbery in Shawan Town, Chongde County, Jiaxing, District Chief Zhou Weilie of the Water Police personally led officers to investigate and pursue the bandits by warship. Recently, he collaborated with the Water Police of the Third District of Wuxing to raid the bandits' hideout. The bandits opened fire and resisted arrest, leading to a fierce battle. In addition to killing several people on the spot, the bandits Zhan and Yang were captured. They are currently being brought back to the district headquarters for strict interrogation.

Ningbo 76

Pirates Plunder and Kidnap People: Around 8:00 PM the other day, over sixty pirates armed with wooden-cased guns arrived in two boats at Zhou Village, Xinyu Zhong Village, Wantang, East Township, Cixi. After landing, they immediately began looting. They first broke into the home of Zhou Guangyu, the village chief, stealing over 1,000 yuan. Next, they robbed the home of Zhou Guangcai, taking over 600 yuan; the home of Shen Wenxing, stealing clothing worth about 100 yuan; the home of Zhou Guangxun, stealing clothing and jewelry worth about 500 yuan; and the home of Zhou Guangzhao, stealing over 200 yuan. Before leaving, they kidnapped the village chief, Zhou Guangyu, and his young son. The looting lasted for three hours before the pirates sailed away towards the East Sea.

Letter Carrier Robbed of Silver Dollars: Ma Chunciao, a letter carrier from Longtai Mound, Fangqiao, Yin County, hired the Ma Shengcai ferry the other day to travel from Ningbo to Miaoyantou. Halfway there, a small boat approached with four bandits on board. They tied up the captain, Ma Heshang, and A Lin, and stole over 900 silver dollars from the letter carrier, Ma Chunciao. After being robbed, the letter carrier immediately returned to Ningbo to report the incident to the Public Security Bureau for investigation, but no arrests have been made.

Five Thousand Farmers Petition the County Government: Over five thousand farmers from the five districts of Yongyi, Haiyan, Fuchang, and Hulong Shiqiao in Cibei petitioned the county government due to landlords such as Ye Xiangsheng, Zhu Weihao, and Li Hongshun arbitrarily reclaiming their land, leaving them with no land to cultivate and creating economic hardship, causing widespread panic. County Magistrate Cheng personally received them on the morning of the day before, explaining that the landlords' unauthorized land reclamation was inappropriate. He immediately issued a public notice prohibiting landlords from arbitrarily raising rents or reclaiming land. The farmers were satisfied and returned to their villages in formation.

Xiaoshan 77

Fire Used to Warm Silkworms Kills Two Children: A farming family named Gao in Xizhuang, Eastern Township, Xiaoshan, raised a large number of silkworms this year. Due to the cold weather, the early silkworms were about to spin their cocoons, and the family used fire for warmth. Around midnight on the 6th, a fire broke out due to negligence in the silkworm-warming stove, quickly destroying two two-story houses, one one-story house, and two thatched sheds, also burning to death two children, aged five and nine. The next morning, the remains were examined, revealing only the pierced lungs and hearts, a pitiful sight.

Unoptimistic Outlook for the Silkworm Season in the Four Rural Areas: There are over twenty cocoon businesses in Toupeng, Nanyang, and other areas of Xiaoshan, which have been leased to companies such as Hangwei Cheng. After the spring silkworms hatched, the weather changed, and recently, as the silkworms approached the big sleep, the weather remained harsh, with continuous rain and unpredictable temperatures. The silkworms were eating wet leaves and suffering from yellow water disease, and their development was uneven. Currently, most of the early silkworms are ready to spin their cocoons, but the late silkworms are just entering the big sleep. Given this situation, it is possible to predict that this year's cocoon production will not be plentiful. As a result, only seven or eight cocoon businesses have been leased out, and the general mood among silkworm farmers is one of worry.

Education News

Important News

Jiangsu Middle School Teachers' Union Petitions the National Assembly 78

Since its establishment, the Jiangsu Middle School Teachers' Union has actively worked to reform and revitalize Jiangsu Province. Now, at the opening of the National Assembly, the union has submitted proposals and sent representatives to Beijing to discuss relevant matters. The submitted documents are listed below.

Document to the National Assembly

Regarding the improvement of education in Jiangsu Province, a draft proposal is respectfully submitted for consideration by the Assembly. We believe that education is the foundation of the nation, the source of vitality, and the determinant of talent and cultural prosperity. Therefore, education should advance with the times, and educational funding should increase annually. With sufficient funding, the education system can be effectively promoted and achieve significant results. According to the Party's program, educational funding should be increased and its independence guaranteed. As the period of political tutelage nears completion and constitutional government is about to begin, the development of education is a matter of utmost urgency for the well-being of the Party's governance and the flourishing of culture. Jiangsu Province is prosperous and populous, and its educational and cultural achievements are among the best in the nation. It now serves as the national capital and the center of the country, and its institutions are closely watched both domestically and internationally. Therefore, it is essential to expand and improve Jiangsu's education system to set an example for the rest of the country and showcase its achievements to the world. The importance of Jiangsu's position and the need to expand and improve its education system cannot be ignored. However, after examining the current state of education in Jiangsu Province, we find that since the reorganization in the sixteenth year of the Republic, the system has suffered a loss of vitality due to the disruptions of the university district system, and its strength has been undermined by the burden of funding the National Central University. Music education continues, but only in form, and the spirit is weary and exhausted. The financial situation is dire and unsustainable. If this continues, not only will it be difficult to achieve new standards, but previous accomplishments may be lost. This is not only a crisis for education in Jiangsu Province but also a threat to the well-being of the nation. We, who are members of the education community in Jiangsu Province, have experienced this firsthand and feel deeply concerned. As your esteemed Assembly opens, we hope that the representatives will engage in insightful discussions and develop grand strategies to benefit the nation and its people. While there are many aspects to consider, the cultivation of culture and academics is a fundamental priority for the nation. Therefore, we hope that the representatives will carefully consider how to expand the education system, increase educational funding, encourage teachers, and improve administration. As the capital of the nation, Jiangsu Province should set a national example. Based on our sincerity, we dare not remain silent. We respectfully offer our humble suggestions as a small contribution. We hereby submit a proposal for improving education in Jiangsu Province. We respectfully request that it be reviewed and approved for submission to the General Assembly for discussion and to establish a clear direction for improving education in Jiangsu Province. We are deeply grateful for your consideration. Respectfully submitted to the National Assembly by Wu Zixiu, Zhang Zhongyou, Wu Dezhang, Zhang Kaixuan, Wu Cangsu, Chen Yue, Xue Jianwu, and 1,006 other faculty members of Jiangsu provincial secondary schools.

Petition Proposals

1. Increase educational funding for Jiangsu Province and ensure its independence. (Reason) In the thirteenth year of the Republic, Jiangsu Province established a special cigarette tax fund for education, collected directly by educational institutions and completely separate from other financial tax revenues. This established Jiangsu's educational funding independence, setting an example for the entire country. However, in the sixteenth year of the Republic, the national government nationalized the cigarette tax and allocated 1.8 million yuan from the province's land tax revenues to compensate. As land tax revenues fluctuate with the harvest, the actual funds received were less than promised, fundamentally undermining Jiangsu's educational funding. From the sixteenth year to the present, counties have accumulated over 2 million yuan in unpaid educational funds. The budget is merely a formality, and loans are not being repaid. Maintaining the current situation is already a challenge, let alone improving and expanding. Even if this limited amount could be fully allocated to Jiangsu's education system, it would barely be enough. However, the national government also assigned Jiangsu the responsibility of funding the National Central University, requiring the province to contribute over 1.3 million yuan annually, which constitutes more than one-third of Jiangsu's total educational funds. This has deprived Jiangsu of its funding sources and increased its financial burden. This is not only unfair compared to other provinces but also contradicts the Ministry of Finance's principle of using provincial taxes to fund provincial schools and national taxes to fund national schools. As a result, Jiangsu bears the empty title of educational funding independence while suffering the actual harm of being cut off and exploited. This year, schools in various provinces have been in session for four months, but Jiangsu has only received one month's worth of funding. The situation is dire. If no remedies are found, the national capital and its leading national and provincial schools will all suffer. We hereby propose two solutions: reducing expenditures and increasing revenue, for your consideration. A. Reduce Expenditures: (1) Eliminate the burden of funding the National Central University. According to the current financial principles of the national government's Ministry of Finance, provincial taxes should fund provincial schools, and national taxes should fund national schools. Therefore, we request that the annual funding of over 1.3 million yuan for the National Central University be shifted to the national tax budget and directly allocated by the Ministry of Finance, thereby relieving Jiangsu's burden and allowing for some expansion. (2) Thoroughly reform the Jiangsu Educational Funding Management Office. The Jiangsu Educational Funding Management Office is responsible for the overall management of educational funding in Jiangsu Province. Strict performance evaluations should be implemented, and a director of the supervisory office should be appointed, with the candidate selected by the education community and appointed by the provincial government. The internal structure of the office should be streamlined, with fewer redundant positions. Supervision should be strengthened, and audits should be thorough. Only in this way can performance be improved and funds be spent wisely. Currently, the director of the management office holds a nominal position and does not handle office affairs personally, leading to an excessive number of redundant staff and widespread corruption. This has caused various rumors and criticisms. As the office is not subject to performance evaluations by the provincial government or oversight by community organizations, the annual waste of funds is likely significant. We request that the Jiangsu Educational Funding Management Office be thoroughly reformed to eliminate waste. B. Increase Revenue: (1) Allocate a percentage of the cigarette tax to compensate for the shortfall in land tax revenues, thereby maintaining Jiangsu's educational funding. On July 2, the sixteenth year of the Republic, members of the Central Executive Committee Wu Zhihui, Li Shizeng, Cai Zimin, and Zhang Jingjiang, along with former Minister of Finance Gu Yingfen and former President of National Central University Zhang Junmou, reached an agreement stating, "If the funds allocated from land tax revenues to educational expenses in each county are insufficient, the Ministry of Finance will allocate the necessary funds from cigarette tax revenues." Currently, the unpaid land tax revenues for education in various counties have reached 2 million yuan over the past three years, while cigarette tax revenues have increased to 10 million yuan. We request that the Ministry of Finance fulfill the original agreement and allocate a percentage of the increased cigarette tax revenues each month to Jiangsu's educational funding. (2) Recover and effectively manage the public forests owned by the Jiangsu Educational Corps to increase production and supplement the province's educational foundation. The establishment of public forests in Jiangsu Province was originally intended to cultivate a foundation for education in the province. Therefore, the operating expenses were initially funded by savings from the regular expenses of various provincial schools. These forests were carefully managed in Jiangpu Laojun for over ten years, and have always been considered as an asset of Jiangsu education. Following the principle of planting trees for ten years, the forests' yields have increased. However, since the reorganization, management has been unclear, and there has been a lack of effective management. Recently, management has been transferred to the Forestry Bureau of the Agricultural and Mining Department. The assets of Jiangsu education have been neglected and encroached upon. We should try to recover and manage these forests, or else sell the property rights at a reasonable price, so the educational funding will slightly increase. (3) Allocate a percentage of the Jiangsu Province's business tax revenues to educational funding. Jiangsu Province's business tax is levied on the developed industry and commerce, so tax revenue will be huge. We request that a percentage of the business tax revenues be allocated annually to Jiangsu's educational funding. Those who take from Jiangsu, must give back to Jiangsu. Because the people of Jiangsu fulfill the obligation of paying tax, the right to receive education, must be planned.

2. Improve the treatment of elementary and secondary school teachers in Jiangsu Province and give them better protection. (Reason) The cost of living continues to rise, especially rapidly in Jiangsu Province in recent years. Educational work is a profession, but the current salary is low, and teachers work diligently all year round. Not enough money to make a living. There is no guarantee for old age, sickness or death, so increasing treatment standard is not enough to maintain a living. Definite protection rules can not give enough incentives. The following methods are used:

(Method) A. Increasing hourly fees. Currently, the salary of secondary school teachers in other provinces is better than in Jiangsu Province. Near by Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Fujian can be used as reference. Because of educational fund shortage in Jiangsu Province, hopes can not be over extended. It is suggested that the monthly salary should be 9 yuan for each hour of teaching in senior high school, and 7 yuan for each hour of teaching in junior high school. This is the lowest limit. This is still less than in other provinces. The monthly salary of staffs, should also be incrementally increased. The standard is being able to work at ease and maintain a living. B. Enact seniority-based salary increase system. Research is central to education. Length of service increases experience and knowledge. Enacting seniority-based salary increases, can relieve living hardships and increase interest in working. It directly benefits the lives of individual and indirectly increases the efficiency of education. C. Children can attend school for free. Secondary school teachers work hard but earn little. They are often unable to afford their children's education because of financial difficulties. There for they loyal to others but struggling to take care of themselves. We should stipulate that all provincial secondary schools will waive tuition and accommodation fees for the children of secondary school teachers, showing respect to teachers. It not only a good rule for teachers, but also show the nation's intention to nurture talent. D. Promulgate regulations on pension and retirement benefits. Teachers serve the society with education as a profession and work hard throughout the year, unable to rest, and have no support for old age, illness, death. Remembering past contributions, the situation is very pitiful. We should clearly stipulate that honoring the old and respecting the wise is also a political achievement of the nation. E. Equip teachers' residences. Teachers are hired from all over the place. At the end of each semester, traveling back and forth on boats and cars, wastes time. Courses and affairs are affected. It is costly for local teacher to come and go from nearby school site. Therefore, schools need to have teachers' residences, teachers can feel more comfortable and work with concentration.

3. Actively promote academic research, cultivate teachers, and improve educational efficiency. (Reason) Most of the faculty members of provincial schools are graduates of universities or specialized schools at home and abroad. They have their own basic knowledge and long-term expertise. Academic research needs to keep up with the times, and more educational teachers should be cultivated. At present, due to limited funds, schools can hardly conduct research activities except for teaching according to chapters and lessons. They are sticking to old ways and culture is falling behind. They are blindly building cars, and more application may be rejected. We should promote academic research to advance culture and pay attention to the cultivation of teachers to innovate education. The following methods are used: A. Stipulate regulations on foreign visits for teachers. After provincial school teachers have served for several years, they should be sent to study in Europe and the United States at public expense in order to improve or sent to foreign countries for visits. They can then use their knowledge to innovate, so that the efficiency of education can be improved day by day. B. Schools should allocate academic research fees and domestic visit fees when preparing the budget. In addition to teaching, various sciences should have deep research and be mutually observed. This will advance education. Current provincial school budgets do not include research fees or domestic visit fees except for salaries and office expenses, so they should be added. C. Hold academic seminars in the summer to develop science and education. Various academic seminars are very popular in Europe, America, and Japan in the summer, so the effectiveness of promoting academic research is significant. Although summer schools are held in various parts of our country, they are limited to the training of young students and lack specialized research in specialized sciences, so there is no opportunity for secondary school teachers to make up for their training. We should organize summer seminars and invite famous scholars from China and abroad to give lectures by division, so that teachers can have a chance to develop their knowledge.

4. Choose wise and capable people carefully, refresh administration, respect teachers, and rectify academic style. Good law must have good personnel and good personnel must have good law. Therefore administration needs to be emphasized. In education, academics should be the focus. Administrative personnel must be reputable in the education community, so they can bring together ideas, do deliberate planning, and use talent. If only people are good at books, signing, running errands, they would flatter those above and look down on those below. Educational offices will be militarized. If academics politicized, then not only will the administration be a state of disarray, but also education will go bankrupt. There will be no standard to abide by. This will cause the province's education to be used to relying on others. The spirit of scholars will be weakened, and the style of learning will be corrupted. I am afraid for the future. We should choose wise and capable people carefully, respect teachers, and rectify academic style in order to increase the efficiency of education and to cultivate the nation's energy.

Santo Tomas Basketball Team Defeats East-West Last Night 84

丨Fifty-Five to Thirty-Four丨The Performance Receives Acclaim Throughout the Arena丨

Departing for Japan Today丨Scheduled to Return to Shanghai on June 12th

The Santo Tomas University basketball team from Manila, Philippines, renowned in the Far East, passed through Shanghai on the Russian Empress last night at 7 PM on their way to a competition in Japan. They depart for Japan today at 9 AM. The Chinese Athletic Association specially invited them to perform a demonstration game, which began at 8:30 PM against the East-West team at the Chinese Basketball Hall. Living up to their reputation, the team defeated the East-West team with their outstanding skills and captivating performance. The score was 55 to 34. The referee was Shen Siliang.

Full Team Roster: Coach Carver, Manager Sevilla, Captain De Rosario, Players Mariano, Silva, Montinola, Jacinto, Villanueva, Biel, Heredia, Reyes, Amayo.

Far Eastern Champions: Four of the ten players are representatives of the Philippine Far Eastern Games basketball team, and are highly acclaimed. The four are Mariano, De Rosario, Jacinto, and Villanueva. Jacinto, the guard, is considered the number one in the Philippines.

Record in the Philippines: This year, the team has fought forty-nine battles, both big and small, in the Philippines, and have been victorious in every one. In the last battle, they lost to the Philippine All-Star team by only one point, with the final score being 42 to 43. In the last three minutes of this game, Santo Tomas was still leading with 42 to 37, but unfortunately, the All-Star team was composed purely of famous Far Eastern athletes from the Philippines, such as Padilla, Salvador, and Schlodohm, all of whom are past Far Eastern athletes from the Philippines.

Motivation for Going to Japan: This trip to Japan is purely voluntary, and Japan has expressed extreme welcome. Japan's recent progress in basketball cannot be measured by ordinary standards, so the team decided to go to Japan for observation. The expenses will be covered by 60% of the ticket sales.

Schedule in Japan: It is planned that there will be a total of eleven matches in Japan. Six matches against the Tokyo Six Universities, two matches against the Osaka Two University teams, two matches against the Two Combined teams, and one match against the Nagoya University team, totaling eleven matches.

Scheduled Return to Shanghai: The team is scheduled to depart for Japan tomorrow at 9 AM on the original ship. They will stay in Japan for twenty-one days and will leave Japan around June 6th, returning to Shanghai around June 12th.

Last Night's Performance: The team's skill last night was praised by all present. They were as light as swallows, not tall but jumping like flying. Every dribble was under their perfect control. Nimble as monkeys, their movements were extremely difficult to predict. Accurate shooting was their forte. Their collaboration was seamless. The communication of the three forwards was sophisticated. The guards were capable of effective support. The substitutes were also all talented players. It was beautiful, it was perfect.

Leadership's Criticism: Santo Tomas coach Carver, who was also a former Far Eastern athlete in the Philippines, told reporters yesterday that the individual skills of the East-West team could be considered not bad. Players like Lu Zhongen, Liang Guoquan, and Wang Xiliang are all outstanding. However, their cooperation is far from satisfactory, and their movements are very slow, giving the opponents time to prepare, which is also a weakness. The forwards attack, but the rear cannot provide support, so many shots rely on individual skills, and the shooting is not accurate. Wen Dingxin is relatively weak in this aspect. In defense, they cannot strictly defend each person, resulting in neglecting the east and losing the west, giving the enemy opportunities. Their team uses five-person defense, and the attack and defense are consistent, which is why they won. It seems that the Chinese team has very little practice time. The failure in the Far East was also due to insufficient preparation compared to Japan, resulting in a disastrous defeat. His words were quite pertinent, worthy of an expert.

Overall Review: The skill was simply divine. After the referee blew the whistle, the center Montinola jumped and tapped the ball, Silva caught it, and after two passes by the guards, it landed in Mariano's hands, who shot and scored immediately, in just a few dozen seconds. The entire arena exclaimed in admiration. Lu Zhongen also scored a basket to show he was not to be outdone. Wen Dingxin scored again, at which time they were leading 4 to 3. Unexpectedly, after that, the Santo Tomas's shots continued to go in, making the score 11 to 4, then 15 to 6. The Chinese team then made a great effort, with Liang Guoquan and Wen Dingxin scoring eight points, chasing the score to 17 to 14, only two points behind. Santo Tomas then substituted Heredia in, and their momentum increased again. The first half ended with 24 to 18, East-West being six points behind. From the start of the second half, the East-West team declined sharply. Wen Dingxin was injured, and Ouyang Yongyuan and Li Baojun were of no help. Finally, they lost with 55 to 24. Track and Field Competition in the Rain 85

Jiangnan Wins Over Baihong

丨Eighty-Six to Seventy-Seven丨

Wang Jihuai Scores Twenty-Three Points, Securing Individual First Place

Decent Results, Track and Field Events Affected by Rain

The track and field competition between the Jiangnan and Baihong teams yesterday resulted in a victory for Jiangnan with a score of 86 to 77. Wang Jihuai of the Jiangnan team secured first place with 23 points. The event began at 2 PM at the Chinese Athletic Field. Unfortunately, the weather did not cooperate, with heavy rain pouring down. However, the athletes from both teams did not let the rain dampen their spirits and continued the competition as scheduled until the end. The referees were soaked to the bone. Students from the Chinese Physical Education School volunteered to assist in the rain, displaying great enthusiasm. Many veterans from both teams did not participate yesterday and served as referees instead. The Baihong team was represented by Chen Xiqiu, Zhou Shaowen, and Dong Zhaobin. The Jiangnan team was represented by He Debao, Long Zexian, Zhang Ming, Wu Jingqi, and Luo Chuanbao. Scoring was based on a 5-3-2-1 system. Datong and Dada Companies' Ships 88

Zhengda and Hanping Collide

Accident Occurred Near Tongzhou the Day Before Yesterday

Both Damaged But Still Sailed Out Yesterday

Passengers Unharmed, Cargo Damaged

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the Zhengda ship of Datong Company and the Hanping ship of Dada Company collided near Longjusha, Xintang, the day before yesterday (the 9th) due to heavy fog. Although the passengers were unharmed, both ships were damaged. The most significant loss among the cargo was fresh eggs, estimated at over 3,600 pieces. Details of the situation are described below:

Circumstances of the Collision: Both the Zhengda and Hanping ships departed from Yangzhou on the morning of the 8th at 10:00 AM. The Zhengda ship was faster than the Hanping. On the 9th, the Zhengda ship was sailing towards Longjusha in Xintang, about seventy or eighty li from Tongzhou, at 3:55 AM. Due to sudden changes in the weather, a thick fog enveloped the area, making it impossible to see even a short distance. It immediately dropped anchor. Around 5:00 AM, the Hanping ship sailed through the waves, approaching Longjusha. It sounded its whistle and prepared to drop anchor at the same location. Suddenly, it heard the chaotic ringing of a bell ahead, realizing that a ship was anchored there. The helmsman was ordered by the second pilot to steer to the right, but the tide was too strong to maneuver. The Zhengda ship's pilot saw the Hanping ship approaching and immediately raised the anchor chain and quickly reversed to avoid it, but it was too late. With a loud crash, the keel of the Zhengda ship broke, and the iron plates cracked. It was temporarily repaired with cloth bags, and the ship barely managed to sail to Shanghai. The Hanping ship had a large hole in its side, but fortunately, it was not seriously damaged and was still able to sail to Shanghai. However, the passengers on both ships were quite frightened.

History of Zhengda and Hanping: The Zhengda ship of Datong Company was built by the Da Zhonghua Shipyard, using a German Meng'am diesel engine, with a load capacity of 1,000 tons. It was launched in July of the 19th year and operated to Yangzhou. The Hanping ship of Dada Company originally belonged to the Hanyeping Ironworks and had a load capacity of over 1,000 tons. It was over ten years old. Later, the factory owed sand taxes to the Hubei Provincial Government and used the ship as collateral. At the end of the 18th year, the provincial government leased it to the Shanghai Yicheng Shipping Company, which operated the Shanghai-Hankou route. In July of the 19th year, Yicheng Company subleased it to Dada Company, changing its route to Yangzhou. Except for the pilot, the captain and crew were not changed.

Losses of Both Ships: Both the Zhengda and Hanping ships arrived in Shanghai around 3:00 PM on the 9th. After investigation, it was found that all 3,460 pieces of fresh eggs on the Zhengda ship, including 1,600 pieces from Maochang, 1,800 pieces from Banda, 100 pieces from Xiehe, 300 pieces from Haining, and 200 pieces from Yihegong, each containing 800 eggs, were broken. The damaged parts of the ship will be inspected by the Da Zhonghua, Ruirong, and Nanyang shipyards. It is estimated that the repair cost will be over 10,000 taels and will take at least twenty days. It should have been docked for repairs immediately, but due to a prior agreement with Catholic devotees to worship the Virgin Mary at Langshan, Tongzhou, it barely managed to sail that evening at 12:00 AM. It will be docked for repairs after returning to Shanghai. The Hanping ship has a large hole in its side, but it is not seriously damaged, so it still sailed to Yangzhou that evening at 12:00 AM. It will also be repaired after returning to Shanghai.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company 91

Pier Five Resumes Normal Work

Organizes a Bonus Campaign Committee

The staff and workers of the CMSNC's No. 5 Pier had no benefits at all from the bonus issued by Li Zhonggong when he left office. Furthermore, they received only a promissory note for their salary arrears in August of last year, which triggered a collective petition to the company. The acting general manager, Song Shuqiao, avoided meeting with them, and the head of the administrative department, Lu Qinghai, made irresponsible perfunctory remarks. The head of the business department, Shen Zhongyi, and the manager of the fourth depot, Sun Jingxiang, made even more excuses, leading to a stalemate. When the No. 5 depot workers began to strike, Shen and Sun became alarmed and invited Yu Xianting, the standing director of the workers' union, to the company for discussions. To protect the overall situation, both parties agreed that Shen and Sun would be responsible for the bonus issue, and they would request the new general manager to achieve this goal. The promissory note for the salary arrears in August will be converted into cash within one or two days. On the other hand, Yu Xianting would be responsible for persuading all the workers to resume work. Therefore, the workers' union convened a meeting that night, and most of the members still insisted on continuing the strike. However, after Yu's earnest explanation and in view of General Manager Guo's imminent assumption of office, they decided that the No. 5 Pier workers would immediately resume normal work and organize a bonus campaign committee to take charge of the process.

Bureau of Social Affairs 94

Prepares to Implement the Factory Law

Dispatches Staff to Inspect Factories Separately

The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, in preparation for the implementation of the Factory Law and its implementing regulations, which the National Government has approved to take effect from August 1, has dispatched staff to various factories for inspection. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency met with Wang Gang, deputy director of the inspection division of the Third Department of the Bureau of Social Affairs, yesterday. He stated that the focus of the factory inspections is on the management and treatment of workers. The focus of the factory surveys conducted by the National Government's Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics, the Ministry of Industry, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, the Transportation University Research Institute, and the Economics Society is on industrial manufacturing aspects, such as raw materials, outputs, and operating machinery. Therefore, the two are actually completely different. The procedure for inspecting factories uses a triplicate notification form. The above-mentioned notification form and the factory's required preparations are sent to the factory in advance. At the designated time, the inspector will hand over the second copy of the notification form to the factory for inspection. It is currently observing various cotton spinning factories.

Silk and Filature Industries Negotiate Public Assessment 95

The settlement between the filature industry and the silk industry has been resolved after several negotiations yesterday. It is rumored that a public assessment has been established. It is understood that the assessment is 1.2 yuan per bolt for Parisian satin, true silk satin-faced brocade crepe, heavy beauty silk, etc., 90 cents per bolt for half-crepe, ordinary beauty silk, etc., 68 cents per bolt for Ti, 40 cents per bolt for Minghua Ge, and 70 cents per bolt for heavy Ge, heavy crepe, heavy plain, Bi factory Ge, Hua silk gauze Luo, line spring, heavy spinning. 60 cents for light crepe, light spinning Hua velvet Ge, light plain Bi, artificial silk Bi crepe, and 56 cents for Hu Qing Ge. True silk true wool Ge is assessed at 1.6 yuan. It is agreed that 16 yards to 25 yards is considered one bolt, 30 yards to 40 yards is considered one and a half bolts, and 40 yards to 50 yards is considered two bolts. It has been submitted to the Bureau of Social Affairs for record. A dispute is finally coming to an end.

Fellow Townsmen from Guangxin 96

Request Suppression of Communist Bandits in Qian and Guang Prefectures

The fellow townsmen's association of the seven counties of Guangxin telegraphed the authorities in Beijing and Jiangxi, stating: "To Commander-in-Chief Chiang, Director He, and Chairman Lu, Fang Zhimin, Shao Wuping, Huang Dao, and other Communist bandits in eastern Jiangxi, recently besieged by the National Army on all sides, and with their food supply cut off, are difficult to sustain. They suddenly led four to five thousand bandits (approximately three thousand armed with rifles and four machine guns) on April 26th to cross the river in the White Sand area of Shangrao by night, passing through the Shixi area of Qianshan, where they were defeated and driven back by the Hu Regiment. They then went to Shitang via Jiudu, Houda, below Tianzhu Rock, pillaging and killing along the way. The devastation is difficult to describe. After arriving in Shitang on the 27th, the district regiments and merchant corps were unable to resist due to their weakness, and either died or fled. District Regiment Chief Ren Fuhan was brutally murdered. The Fang bandits then intercepted all the important locations on all sides, and the merchants in the city were left to be slaughtered. District Chief Zeng Xingsan and wealthy merchants, both men and women, were mostly abducted, with many being brutally killed on the spot. No store, whether large or small, was spared. The losses in Shitang amounted to no less than several million, truly a great catastrophe. On the 29th, the Fang bandits entered Wenlin Pass from Shitang, and a portion entered Chong'an County, Fujian Province, via Heshangping into Fenwater Pass, approximately using the mountains on the Jiangxi-Fujian border as their nest. The local bandit Wang Mingui of Shitang, Qianshan, began to plunder and pillage ten li outside the city in Qidu on the day the Hu Regiment returned to Hekou, and has recently become even more rampant. Wang's banditry has not been eradicated, and now it is further compounded by the large force of Fang and Shao hiding along the Fujian border, forming a desperate alliance. The situation in Qianshan is unimaginable. Fang and Shao's bandits have been entrenched in Yiheng for over two years, amassing losses and destroying counties, and the three counties of Gui, Yi, and Heng have become a desolate wasteland, a heartbreaking sight. Now that Fang and Shao's bandits have changed their direction, using the Fujian border of Qianshan and Guangfeng counties as their base, the suppression will be even more difficult than before. The two counties of Qian and Guang will become the continuation of Yiheng. The thought of it sends chills down the spine. Xu Xun and others are heartbroken for their hometown and dare not remain silent. They have detailed the facts and tearfully reported, earnestly begging you to order the dispatch of elite troops to Qianshan to encircle and thoroughly suppress the bandits, eradicating them completely, and to request that the Fujian Provincial Government dispatch troops to launch a fierce attack, annihilating them in the shortest possible time. This is the tearful plea of the people of Guangxin. Your Excellencies, with your compassion for the suffering, will surely heed the voice of the people, dispatch elite troops, and set a time limit for the suppression. Guangxin will be fortunate, and the Party and the nation will be fortunate. We cannot express our gratitude enough. Xu Xun, Guo Tong, and Liu Lianghan, Standing Committee members of the Shanghai Fellow Townsmen Association of the seven counties of Guangxin, bow in supplication, "Best regards."
